-- Person(id, firstname, lastname, year_of_birth, country_id)
-- friendship(person1_id, person2_id, friends_since)
-- follow(person_id, followed_person_id, follows_since)
SELECT *
FROM person
JOIN follow ON (person.id = follow.person_id)
